Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists of Grand Prix Birmingham 2017
================================================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on August 12, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











The main event may have only started this Saturday morning, but the action already began on Friday. Naturally, we were most interested in the Last-Chance Trials run that day, as those results actually influenced the Grand Prix itself, awarding byes to all the winners for one thing. Plus, these people's decklists provided a first idea of what to expect over the course of the weekend ...


Of course, with a format like Modern, famous for its vast wealth of varying while veritably viable strategies, the best conclusion one could draw from the winning decklists likely was: You better come prepared for just about anything!







#### Daniel Ghaffarpour, Grand Prix Trial Winner


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
